 Chalisa is a prayer made in simple language by the devotee to please his God or isht and to solve his problems
 isko chalisa isliye kehete hai kyonki isamen chalis line hoti hai
 Being written in simple language, it can be read easily, so it became very popular in the public
 iske paath ke liye kisi khaas niyam kii aavashyaktaa nahin hoti he lekin kuch choti-choti baton kaa dhyaan rakhana jaruri he
 Different lines have different importance in Chalisa and they have special use in special problems
 tulsidas ji dwaara likhi huyi hanuman chalisa sarvaadhik shaktishaalee or lokapriy maani jaati he
 Use the method of Hanuman Chalisa - Establish a picture of Lord Hanuman and his favorite Shri Rama
 iske baad unke samaksh jal se bharaa patr rakhen
 Read Chalisa at least 3 times to 108 times
 paath ke uparaant us jal ko prasad kii tarah grahan karen
 Try that the time of chalisa recitation is same daily
 vishesh dashaon main yatra tathaa sote samay bhi chalisa kaa paath kar sakate hai

 He never said that she was dating Arjun
 centre sarkaar jald hi kaarobaariyon par 15 se 25 lakh yaa usase kam rakam ke jurmaane ke cese waapas legi
 All these cases are pending before the court
 iske liye chah maah kii samay seemaa nirdhaarit kii gai he
 Union Finance Minister Piyush Goyal gave this information at a program of Chamber of Commerce in Raipur on Monday
 isaki jagah par nai darentay kii gai hai
 Goyal said that more than the fine amount is being spent in legal advice and fighting the case in court
 isliye aise maamalon ko waapas lenaa hi munasib samajha ja rahaa he
 He told that most of the cases are going on in the Supreme Court
 kendriya vitt mantri piyush goyal ne kaha ki mantralay ne is par kanoonee salaah lene ke saath hi aise prakarnon kii suchi taiyaar karne kaa kaam shuru kar diya he
 He claimed that this move of the government would reduce the number of such pending cases in the Supreme Court from 40 to 50 per cent
 unke mutabik isse sarkaar or kaarobaariyon ko badi raahat milegi
 This will be the new system Minister Piyush Goyal said that till now the government used to go to court for any amount, but now a new system is being made
 unhone bataaya ki nai vyavastha ke tahat 25 lakh tak ke jurmaane vaale maamalon main centre sarkaar tribunel main apil karegi
